SELECT TOP # fld.run, fld.avg_sky_muJy, fld.runarea AS area, ISNULL(fp.nfirstmatch,#)  FROM (   SELECT run, sum(primaryArea) AS runarea,  #e6*avg(power(cast(#. as float),#*sky_r)) as avg_sky_muJy  FROM Field  GROUP BY run  ) AS fld  LEFT OUTER JOIN (   SELECT p.run, count(*) AS nfirstmatch  FROM FIRST AS fm  INNER JOIN photoprimary as p  ON p.objid=fm.objid  GROUP BY p.run  ) AS fp  ON fld.run=fp.run  ORDER BY fld.run

SELECT p.ra,p.dec,p.u,p.g,p.r,p.i,p.z,   --for the definition of rating used here, see Creaner et al, #, The Locus Algorithm: A technique for identifying optimised pointings for differential photometry   (#-abs(((p.g-@g_target)-((p.r-@r_target)))/@col_limit))*(#-abs(((p.r-@r_target)-((p.i-@i_target)))/@col_limit)) as rating        -- from the Photometric Objects Catalogue FROM PhotoObjAll AS p     WHERE    (     -- Reference in a FoV centred on the pointing      p.ra BETWEEN (@point_ra-(@fov_ra/#))  AND (@point_ra+(@fov_ra/#))      AND p.dec BETWEEN (@point_dec-(@fov/#)) AND (@point_dec+(@fov/#))   )    AND    (     -- Reference passes the Clean Sample of Point Sources tests 	((p.status & #)!=#)  	AND ((p.flags & #)!=#)  	AND ((p.flags & #)=#)  	AND (p.type = #)    )    AND    (     -- Reference magnitude is in the correct range 	p.r BETWEEN (@r_target-@mag_limit) AND (@r_target+@mag_limit)   )    AND    (     -- Reference colour is in the correct range 		(p.g - p.r) BETWEEN ((@g_target-@r_target)-@col_limit)AND((@g_target-@r_target)+@col_limit) 	AND 		(p.r - p.i) BETWEEN ((@r_target-@i_target)-@col_limit)AND((@r_target-@i_target)+@col_limit)   )         ORDER BY rating DESC

SELECT up_id,  dbo.fGetNearestObjIdEq( up_ra,up_dec,up_sep ) as objId   FROM #upload  WHERE  dbo.fGetNearestObjIdEq( up_ra,up_dec,up_sep ) IS NOT NULL  SELECT TOP #   p.ra,p.dec, p.run,p.rerun,p.camCol,p.field,p.obj,p.r,ISNULL(s.class,#) as class,ISNULL(s.subClass,#) as subClass  FROM ..PhotoObj AS p  LEFT OUTER JOIN ..SpecObj s ON p.objID = s.bestObjID  JOIN #x AS x ON x.objID=p.objID  JOIN #upload AS u ON u.up_id = x.up_id   WHERE  ( p.type = # OR p.type = #)   ORDER BY x.up_id
SELECT TOP #  star.apogee_id, star.ra, star.dec, star.glon, star.glat,   star.vhelio_avg, star.vscatter,  obj.j, obj.h, obj.k, obj.ak_targ, obj.ak_targ_method, obj.ak_wise,  aspcap.teff, aspcap.logg, aspcap.param_m_h FROM apogeeStar star  JOIN aspcapStar aspcap on aspcap.apstar_id = star.apstar_id  JOIN apogeeObject obj on aspcap.target_id = obj.target_id WHERE (aspcap.aspxcapflag & dbo.fApogeeAspcapFlag(&&&)) = # and aspcap.teff > #  and (star.vhelio_avg > #) and (star.starflag &  dbo.fApogeeStarFlag(&&&)) = #  and star.nvisits > # order by aspcap.apogee_id
SELECT    s.BESTOBJID, s.RA, s.DEC, s.Z, p.modelMag_r, p.psffwhm_r, p.extinction_r into specTable from specObj AS s LEFT OUTER JOIN PhotoPrimary AS p ON s.BESTOBJID = p.objID Where      (s.CLASS = &&&)
SELECT    s.BESTOBJID, s.PLUG_RA, s.PLUG_DEC, s.Z, s.Z_ERR, s.RCHI2, p.modelMag_r, p.psffwhm_r, p.extinction_r into specTable from specObj AS s LEFT OUTER JOIN PhotoPrimary AS p ON s.BESTOBJID = p.objID Where      (s.CLASS = &&&)
